Part REF-W29: ARC-AGI-1 Wave 29 Rules and Acceptance Criteria

Wave 29 adds 18 new arc_transform/3 rules and four helper predicates to arc_benchmark.pl in the Mentova repository, raising the benchmark score from 236/400 = 59.00% to 242/400 = 60.50% (Run 43, Attempt 29).

The 18 new rules are:

draw_x_diagonals: The grid contains exactly one nonzero cell at (SR, SC) with value SV. The output places SV at every cell (R, C) where |R-SR| = |C-SC| (the two diagonal lines through the source cell), and 0 elsewhere. Task solved: 623ea044.

fill_frame_gaps: Rows with 4 or more nonzero cells are frame rows; columns with 4 or more nonzero cells are frame columns. Zero cells in frame rows are filled with 2 between the global minimum and maximum nonzero column. Zero cells in frame columns are filled with 2 between the global minimum and maximum nonzero row. Task solved: 4612dd53.

scale_stamp_at_2_markers: The input has a template region containing 1-cells and 2-marker cells adjacent to the 1-cells, plus isolated NxN blocks of 2-cells (not adjacent to any 1-cell). The relative offsets of the 1-cells and template 2-cells are computed from the minimum template-2 anchor. The isolated blocks determine N. For K=1 template-2 marker, each isolated block is stamped with the 1-shape scaled to N. For K=2 template-2 markers, pairs of isolated blocks whose relative position matches the template-2 relative position are found, and the 1-shape is stamped from the anchor block. Task solved: 447fd412.

four_way_reflect: The color with the most nonzero cells is the main color (ties broken by lowest value); the other nonzero color is the marker. The bounding box of marker cells determines a center: SumR2 = MarkerMinR + MarkerMaxR, SumC2 = MarkerMinC + MarkerMaxC. Each main-color cell at (R, C) is also reflected to (R, SumC2-C), (SumR2-R, C), and (SumR2-R, SumC2-C), all clipped to grid bounds. Tasks solved: 4938f0c2, 4c5c2cf0.

replace_minority_with_5: The nonzero color with the most cells is the background color. All other nonzero cells become 5. Zero cells remain 0. Helper arc_w29_max_count_col/2 finds the majority color; on ties the lower value wins. Task solved: 9565186b (already solved by pre-existing rule keep_majority_color; wave 29 provides alternative implementation).

diagonal_pair_8corners: Connected components that form NxN squares are identified by helper arc_w29_cc_is_square/4. Pairs of same-N squares whose top-left corners differ by exactly N in both row and column (diagonal spacing) are found. For each such pair at (R1,C1) and (R2,C2), NxN blocks of 8s are stamped at the virtual corners: position (2*R1-R2, 2*C2-C1) and (2*R2-R1, 2*C1-C2), each clipped to grid bounds. Task solved: 22233c11.

extend_rect_to_8: A single 8-cell exists outside a rectangular frame. The frame's bounding box is computed from nonzero non-8 cells. The outer color (from border cells) and inner color (from interior cells) are identified. The 8-cell's position determines the extension direction: if 8 is above the frame, the frame's top row extends up to include the 8-cell's row; similarly for below, left, and right. The extended bounding box is filled: border cells get outer color, interior cells get inner color. Task solved: b548a754 (already solved by pre-existing rule extend_rect_toward_8; wave 29 provides alternative implementation).

gravity_down (shift variant): Each nonzero cell at row R shifts to row R+1. The top row becomes all zeros. This differs from the pre-existing gravity_down (which moves cells all the way to the bottom of the column). Task solved: 25ff71a9.

connected_groups_to_8: 4-connected components of nonzero cells with more than one cell are recolored to 8. Isolated single-cell components retain their original color. Task solved: 67385a82 (already solved by pre-existing rule recolor_multi_cell_comps_to_8; wave 29 provides alternative implementation).

rotate_90ccw: 90-degree counter-clockwise rotation. The output grid has NC rows and NR columns. Output cell (R, C) gets the value from input cell (C, NR-R+1). Task solved: ed36ccf7 (already solved by pre-existing rule rotate_90_ccw; wave 29 provides alternative implementation).

mark_5_with_other: The grid contains one non-5 nonzero color OC and some 5-cells. The output places OC at each cell where the input had 5, and 0 everywhere else. Task solved: f76d97a5 (already solved by pre-existing rule swap_5_with_other; wave 29 provides alternative implementation).

erase_diagonals_from_hole: The grid has exactly one 0-cell (hole) at (HR, HC). Each cell (R, C) where |R-HR| = |C-HC| is set to 0; all other cells retain their original values. Task solved: ea786f4a (already solved by pre-existing rule diagonal_zero_from_center; wave 29 provides alternative implementation).

isolated_cells_to_1: 4-connected components of nonzero cells with exactly one cell (isolated cells) are recolored to 1. All other cells retain their original values. Task solved: aedd82e4 (already solved by pre-existing rule isolated_to_1; wave 29 provides alternative implementation).

five_col_to_row_color: Each row containing a 5-cell is identified; the column of the 5 determines the fill color via a fixed mapping (column 1 -> 2, column 2 -> 4, column 3 -> 3). The entire row is filled with that color. Helper arc_w29_col_color/2 stores the mapping. Task solved: a85d4709 (already solved by pre-existing rule col5_to_row_color; wave 29 provides alternative implementation).

count_ones_fill: The total number of 1-cells is counted. That many 2-cells are placed starting in row 1 left-to-right, then rows 2+ in center-outward column order (center = NC//2+1, alternating right and left offsets). All other cells become 0. Task solved: 794b24be (already solved by pre-existing rule count_cells_to_canonical_3x3; wave 29 provides alternative implementation).

color_count_to_diagonal: The number of distinct values in the grid determines the output pattern on a square grid: 1 distinct value -> row 1 filled with 5s; 2 distinct values -> main diagonal (R=C) filled with 5s; 3 or more distinct values -> anti-diagonal (R+C=NR+1) filled with 5s. All other cells become 0. Task solved: 6e02f1e3 (already solved by pre-existing rule grid_3x3_row_pattern_to_diagonal; wave 29 provides alternative implementation).

shift_8_down_1: Each 8-cell at (R, C) produces a 2 at (R+1, C). All other output cells are 0. Task solved: a79310a0 (already solved by pre-existing rule shift_down_8_to_2; wave 29 provides alternative implementation).

fill_row_gap_ones: In each row, when the pattern 1,0,1 appears at positions (C, C+1, C+2), the zero at C+1 is replaced by 2. All other cells retain their original values. Task solved: a699fb00 (already solved by pre-existing rule fill_row_span_with_2; wave 29 provides alternative implementation).

Helper predicates added in wave 29:

arc_w29_max_count_col/2: Given a list of color values, returns the color with the most occurrences. On ties, the lower color value wins. Uses msort/sort to count occurrences and min_list to break ties.

arc_w29_cc_is_square/4: Given a list of component(Color, Cells) terms, backtracks through components checking whether the cells form an NxN square. Returns the top-left corner (TL_R, TL_C) and side length N. Used by diagonal_pair_8corners and scale_stamp_at_2_markers.

arc_w29_iso_sq_cc/5: Finds isolated NxN square components of color 2 (not adjacent to template-2 cells) in the component list. Returns top-left and N.

arc_w29_col_color/2: Three-clause fact mapping column index (1-indexed) to fill color: 1->2, 2->4, 3->3.

Net new solves in wave 29: 6 tasks (623ea044, 4612dd53, 447fd412, 4938f0c2, 4c5c2cf0, 22233c11). The remaining 13 target tasks were already solved by earlier-wave rules under different names; the wave 29 implementations provide alternative Prolog clauses.

Acceptance criteria for wave 29:

AC-W29-001: arc_transform(draw_x_diagonals, ...) matches all training pairs of task 623ea044.
AC-W29-002: arc_transform(fill_frame_gaps, ...) matches all training pairs of task 4612dd53.
AC-W29-003: arc_transform(scale_stamp_at_2_markers, ...) matches all training pairs of task 447fd412.
AC-W29-004: arc_transform(four_way_reflect, ...) matches all training pairs of tasks 4938f0c2 and 4c5c2cf0.
AC-W29-005: arc_transform(diagonal_pair_8corners, ...) matches all training pairs of task 22233c11.
AC-W29-006: All wave 29 arc_transform clauses end with ! and include NR =< 30, NC =< 30 size guards.
AC-W29-007: Full 400-task benchmark completes within 600 seconds. Score 242/400 = 60.50% confirmed.

Score improvement: 236/400 = 59.00% to 242/400 = 60.50% (+6 tasks).

Status as of 2026-06-18: COMPLETE. Wave 29 merged on Mentova PR #38. Score: 242/400 = 60.50%.


WAVE 30 RULES (Run 44, 251/400 = 62.75%)

Nine new arc_transform/3 clauses and two new helpers were added to arc_benchmark.pl raising the score from 242/400 (60.50%) to 251/400 (62.75%). All 9 rules solve previously unsolved tasks.

Rule descriptions:

fill_2cluster_bbox_with_4: The grid contains sparse 2-cells grouped in space. Cells within Chebyshev distance 2 of each other belong to the same cluster (helper arc_cheby2_cc/2 implements BFS with max(|dr|,|dc|) <= 2 connectivity). For each cluster, the bounding box is computed; non-zero, non-2 cells inside the bbox are set to 4. Task solved: 36fdfd69.

reflect_fives_through_2frame: The 2-cells form a rectangular frame. The bounding box of all 2-cells defines the frame [FrMinR, FrMaxR, FrMinC, FrMaxC]. Each 4-connected component of 5-cells is erased and reflected through the nearest frame wall. If the CC is above the frame (MaxR5 < FrMinR), each cell (R, C) maps to (2*FrMinR - R, C); if below (MinR5 > FrMaxR), maps to (2*FrMaxR - R, C); if left (MaxC5 < FrMinC), maps to (R, 2*FrMinC - C); else maps to (R, 2*FrMaxC - C). Out-of-bounds reflected cells are dropped. Task solved: 6855a6e4.

replace_1s_in_8bbox_with_3: The bounding box of all 8-cells is computed. Every 1-cell whose position falls inside this box is changed to 3. All other cells are unchanged. Task solved: 32597951.

add_3border_4fill_to_6shapes: For each 4-connected region of 6-cells, the bounding box is found. A 3-border is drawn one cell outside the bbox (non-6 cells at that border become 3, overwriting 8s and other colors). Any 8-cell inside the bbox becomes 4. Interior overwrites border when both conditions apply. Task solved: 543a7ed5.

complete_band_through_crossing: A row or column is a "band" if it contains exactly 2 distinct non-zero colors. For each such band, the dominant color (more cells) fills all positions holding the minority color. Column fixes take priority over row fixes at the same cell. Task solved: ba97ae07.

shoot_isolated_into_8block: The bounding box of 8-cells defines a block. Isolated non-0, non-8 cells shoot rays toward the block. A cell in the row range of the block shoots horizontally; a cell in the column range shoots vertically. The first 8-cell hit in the block (scanning inward from the block edge) takes the shooter's color. Task solved: 1f642eb9.

extend_marker_from_arrow: Exactly two non-zero colors exist. The color with exactly 1 cell is the marker; the color with the most cells is the arrow body. The direction from marker to arrow centroid determines orientation (horizontal if |DC| >= |DR|, vertical otherwise). The marker color is extended in the opposite direction (away from the arrow), filling 0-cells beyond the arrow's far edge. Task solved: 25d487eb.

fill_8block_by_quadrant: The bounding box of 8-cells defines a block with center (CenR, CenC). Each isolated non-0, non-8 cell at (IR, IC) is erased; its color is placed at the 8-block corner nearest its quadrant. If IR < CenR, target row is MinR8; else MaxR8. If IC < CenC, target col is MinC8; else MaxC8. Task solved: d89b689b.

remove_stray_cells: Any non-zero cell with fewer than 2 same-color 4-connected neighbors is erased (set to 0). The check uses the original input grid (single pass). This removes isolated or singly-connected "stray" cells while preserving rectangular or well-connected shapes. Task solved: 7f4411dc.

Helper predicates added in wave 30:

arc_cheby2_cc/2: Takes a list of R-C cells and returns a list of Chebyshev-2 connected components. Two cells are in the same component when they are reachable via a chain where each step has max(|dr|,|dc|) <= 2.

arc_cheby2_expand/4: BFS worker for arc_cheby2_cc/2. Queue = cells to expand; Unvis = remaining unvisited cells. At each step, finds all cells in Unvis within Cheby-2 of the head cell, adds them to the queue and removes them from Unvis.

Acceptance criteria for wave 30:

AC-W30-001: arc_transform(fill_2cluster_bbox_with_4, ...) matches all training pairs of task 36fdfd69.
AC-W30-002: arc_transform(reflect_fives_through_2frame, ...) matches all training pairs of task 6855a6e4.
AC-W30-003: arc_transform(replace_1s_in_8bbox_with_3, ...) matches all training pairs of task 32597951.
AC-W30-004: arc_transform(add_3border_4fill_to_6shapes, ...) matches all training pairs of task 543a7ed5.
AC-W30-005: arc_transform(complete_band_through_crossing, ...) matches all training pairs of task ba97ae07.
AC-W30-006: arc_transform(shoot_isolated_into_8block, ...) matches all training pairs of task 1f642eb9.
AC-W30-007: arc_transform(extend_marker_from_arrow, ...) matches all training pairs of task 25d487eb.
AC-W30-008: arc_transform(fill_8block_by_quadrant, ...) matches all training pairs of task d89b689b.

SECTION REF-W31 - WAVE 31 ARC-AGI-1 NAMED RULES (v22 addition)

Wave 31 adds five new named rules to arc_benchmark.pl in the Mentova repository and four supporting helper predicates. The wave corrects a systemic 0-vs-1-indexing bug found in all five rules: arc_grid_at uses nth1 (1-based indexing), but the wave 31 code was written with 0-based between/3 ranges and numlist/3 calls. All five rules and all four helpers were corrected to use 1-indexed coordinates throughout.

New helpers:

arc_w31_greedy_3x3/3 - greedily selects non-overlapping 3x3 block top-left corners from a sorted candidate list; two candidates overlap when their row or column distance is less than 3.

arc_w31_bfs2cc/6 - BFS over 4-connected cells of value 2; bounds check uses R >= 1, R =< NR, C >= 1, C =< NC.

arc_w31_expand_right/5 - scans right while arc_grid_at returns 2; stop condition is C+1 > NC (1-indexed: C1 =< NC).

arc_w31_expand_down/6 - scans down while the full column span remains 2; stop condition is R+1 > NR (1-indexed: R1 =< NR).

New rules:

stamp_1234_around_5_blocks (task 95990924): Locates all 2x2 blocks of 5s. For each block with top-left at (BR, BC), places marker 1 at (BR-1, BC-1), 2 at (BR-1, BC+2), 3 at (BR+2, BC-1), 4 at (BR+2, BC+2), subject to grid bounds.

fill_3x3_zero_blocks_with_1 (task 6cf79266): Finds all 3x3 all-zero blocks; applies arc_w31_greedy_3x3 to select non-overlapping ones in scan order; fills selected blocks with value 1.

fill_below_shape_by_color_count (task fcc82909): Finds canonical 2x2 non-zero shapes (top-left anchored: cell above and cell to the left must be 0). Counts unique colors SN in the 2x2 block. Fills the two columns of the block for SN rows below the block bottom with value 3.

fill_horiz_gap_with_9 (task ef135b50): Identifies solid 2-rectangles by top-left expansion. For each pair A (left) and B (right) with non-empty row overlap and column gap, and no blocking rectangle in between, fills the row-overlap x column-gap region with value 9.

draw_3_frame_around_2_clusters (task b27ca6d3): BFS identifies connected components of 2-cells with at least 2 cells. For each cluster, finds all cells one step outside the bounding box (the frame). Fills zero frame cells with value 3.

Acceptance criteria for wave 31:

AC-W31-001: arc_transform(stamp_1234_around_5_blocks, ...) matches all training pairs of task 95990924.
AC-W31-002: arc_transform(fill_3x3_zero_blocks_with_1, ...) matches all training pairs of task 6cf79266.
AC-W31-003: arc_transform(fill_below_shape_by_color_count, ...) matches all training pairs of task fcc82909.
AC-W31-004: arc_transform(fill_horiz_gap_with_9, ...) matches all training pairs of task ef135b50.
AC-W31-005: arc_transform(draw_3_frame_around_2_clusters, ...) matches all training pairs of task b27ca6d3.
AC-W31-006: All wave 31 arc_transform clauses end with ! and include NR =< 30, NC =< 30 size guards.
AC-W31-007: Full 400-task benchmark completes within 600 seconds. Score 256/400 = 64.00% confirmed.

Score improvement: 251/400 = 62.75% to 256/400 = 64.00% (+5 tasks).

SECTION REF-W32 - WAVE 32 ARC-AGI-1 NAMED RULES (v23 addition)

Wave 32 adds six new named rules to arc_benchmark.pl in the Mentova repository and four supporting helper predicates. All six rules were verified against full training data before insertion. Task 1b2d62fb was already solved by an existing rule (left_right_at_1col_sep_nor_to_8); the remaining five tasks are net new wins.

New helpers:

arc_w32_bfs_val/7 - BFS over 4-connected cells of a given value V; accumulates visited cells in Vis; terminates when the queue is empty. Used by arc_w32_val_comps.

arc_w32_collect_comps/7 - iterates over all seed cells of value V; for each unseen seed, calls arc_w32_bfs_val to collect the full connected component; accumulates components in result list.

arc_w32_val_comps/5 - wrapper that collects all cells of value V with findall, then calls arc_w32_collect_comps with an empty Seen list.

arc_w32_rank_sizes/3 - converts a sorted-descending list of component sizes to size-rank pairs starting at rank 1; used by color_5_comps_by_size.

New rules:

assemble_3x3_from_5_anchors (task 137eaa0f): Finds all 5-valued anchor cells. Collects neighbor offsets DR-DC-V for non-zero, non-5 cells adjacent to any anchor. Assembles a 3x3 output with value 5 at center (2,2) and each offset filled from collected pieces.

scale_5x5_by_color_count (task 469497ad): Counts unique non-zero colors K in a 5x5 input. Scales the grid K-fold to produce a K*5 x K*5 output. Cells from non-zero source tiles copy their value; scaled zero regions with diagonal offsets receive value 2 at four corner positions.

extract_5frame_with_interior_8s (task 3f7978a0): Finds left and right columns containing 5-valued cells. Identifies the bounding rows of those cells. Expands one row above and below to find 8-corner cells. Extracts a frame where borders are 5 or 8 and interior 8s are preserved.

unique_color_region (task 0b148d64): Finds the two colors in a binary-color grid. Computes connected components for each color. Selects the color with fewer components (the unique-component side). Crops the bounding box of that color's cells.

mark_shared_zero_across_1_divider (task 1b2d62fb): Finds the column DC that contains only 1s (the divider). Verifies the left half-width equals the right half-width. For each row, checks whether the left-half cell and its mirror on the right are both 0; if so, marks the output cell 8; otherwise 0.

color_5_comps_by_size (task 6e82a1ae): Finds all connected components of 5-valued cells. Ranks them by size descending (largest = rank 1). Assigns each component's rank as the new color value. Non-5 cells keep their original value.

Acceptance criteria for wave 32:

AC-W32-001: arc_transform(assemble_3x3_from_5_anchors, ...) matches all training pairs of task 137eaa0f.
AC-W32-002: arc_transform(scale_5x5_by_color_count, ...) matches all training pairs of task 469497ad.
AC-W32-003: arc_transform(extract_5frame_with_interior_8s, ...) matches all training pairs of task 3f7978a0.
AC-W32-004: arc_transform(unique_color_region, ...) matches all training pairs of task 0b148d64.
AC-W32-005: arc_transform(mark_shared_zero_across_1_divider, ...) matches all training pairs of task 1b2d62fb.
AC-W32-006: arc_transform(color_5_comps_by_size, ...) matches all training pairs of task 6e82a1ae.
AC-W32-007: All wave 32 arc_transform clauses end with ! and include NR =< 30, NC =< 30 size guards.
AC-W32-008: Full 400-task benchmark completes within 600 seconds. Score 261/400 = 65.25% confirmed.

Wave 33 adds four new named rules solving four previously unsolved ARC-AGI-1 tasks.

Rules and tasks solved:

fill_8shape_bbox_gaps_with_2 (task 6d75e8bb): Finds the global column bounding box [MinC, MaxC] of all 8-valued cells. For each row that contains any 8-cell, fills all 0-cells within [MinC, MaxC] with value 2.

extend_l_shape_diagonal (task 6e19193c): Finds all 3-cell L-shaped connected components. For each L-shape, identifies the corner cell (adjacent to both endpoints), computes the diagonal extension direction (sum of the two arm directions), and paints cells from corner+2*ext_dir onward (skipping the outer-corner cell) until the grid boundary, using the shape color. Helper: arc_w33_diag_cells/7.

strip_8fill_with_4 (task 673ef223): Locates two opposing vertical edge-strips of 2s (one on the left edge col 1, one on the right edge col NC). Determines which strip is "active" (contains interior 8-cells). For each active-strip row with an 8 at column C: replaces the 8 with 4 and fills from the strip edge inward to C-1 (or C+1) with 8s. The "passive" strip row at the same index within its strip is then filled entirely (except the strip cell itself) with 8s.

replace_5sep_match_with_5 (task 63613498): Finds an L-shaped separator of 5s: col SC rows 1..SR and row SR cols 1..SC (corner at (SR,SC)). Classifies non-background components as "adjacent" if all cells lie in Q1 (row < SR, col < SC) or "non-adjacent" otherwise. Normalizes each component's cell pattern relative to its minimum bounding corner. For each non-adjacent component whose normalized pattern matches any adjacent component's pattern, overwrites that component with 5s.

Acceptance criteria for wave 33:

AC-W33-003: arc_transform(strip_8fill_with_4, ...) matches all training pairs of task 673ef223.
AC-W33-004: arc_transform(replace_5sep_match_with_5, ...) matches all training pairs of task 63613498.
AC-W33-005: All wave 33 arc_transform clauses end with ! and include NR =< 30, NC =< 30 size guards.

WAVE 41 RULE ADDITIONS (2026-06-19)

Four new arc_transform rules added to arc_benchmark.pl in Mentova repo, feature/arc-wave41 branch.

Rules added:

l_path_2to3 (task a2fd1cf0): exactly two non-zero cells (one color 2, one color 3); draws an L-path of color 8 with corner at (row_of_2, col_of_3); horizontal arm in row of dot-2 (excluding dot-2 col), vertical arm in col of dot-3 (excluding both dot rows); variant of l_path_connect with different endpoint and path colors.

eject_corner_markers (task 952a094c): a hollow rectangular frame of one color encloses exactly four non-zero cells at the four interior corners; the four corner markers are removed and placed at the four exterior corners of the frame in a 180-degree rotation: interior top-left -> exterior bottom-right, interior top-right -> exterior bottom-left, interior bottom-left -> exterior top-right, interior bottom-right -> exterior top-left.

self_similar_tile (task 8f2ea7aa): all non-zero cells share one color and form a shape with a bounding box of size BS_R x BS_C; the grid is exactly BS_R x BS_C blocks wide and tall; each meta-block position (DR, DC) that matches a relative cell of the shape gets a copy of the shape; the shape tiles itself at the block positions defined by its own relative cell pattern.

attract_to_center (task ae3edfdc): cells with a singleton color (appearing exactly once) act as attractors; for each attractor, the associated main color has all its cells in the same row or same column as the attractor; each main-color cell moves one step toward the attractor (to the orthogonal neighbor on the attractor's side); the original cell is cleared; the attractor itself is unchanged.

Acceptance criteria for wave 41:
AC-W41-001: arc_transform(l_path_2to3, ...) matches all training pairs of task a2fd1cf0.
AC-W41-002: arc_transform(eject_corner_markers, ...) matches all training pairs of task 952a094c.
AC-W41-003: arc_transform(self_similar_tile, ...) matches all training pairs of task 8f2ea7aa.

WAVE 42 RULE ADDITIONS (2026-06-19)

Thirteen new arc_transform rules added to arc_benchmark.pl in Mentova repo, feature/arc-wave42 branch. Twelve of thirteen fired in benchmark Run 51.

Rules added:

inner_gap_fill (task d6ad076f): finds a single-color non-zero rectangle with a 1-cell inner border of non-zero cells and a zero-cell interior region; fills the zero interior with the border color.

extract_bounded_subgrid (target task not confirmed in run 51 - rule added but did not fire): extracts a bounded rectangular subgrid by finding non-zero bounding box coordinates and cropping to that region.

fill_periodic_holes (task 484b58aa): detects periodic pattern period P from repeating rows or columns; fills zero-valued cells that fall on a periodic position with the expected periodic value.

fill_max_zero_cross (task 2bee17df): finds the row and column with the most zero cells; fills those row/column cells with the non-zero value found at their intersection or dominant color.

two_to_wall_expand (task ecdecbb3): connected components of value 2 expand outward in each cardinal direction until they hit a non-zero wall or grid edge; the expansion path is filled with value 2.

color_5_by_stripe (task c9f8e694): horizontal or vertical stripes of 5s are recolored according to a color key derived from non-5 markers in the grid; each 5-stripe's color is determined by the nearest marker.

max_color_columns (task a3325580): finds the columns that contain the maximum count of non-zero cells; output marks those columns with a distinct value.

expand_2_in_3_blob (task b527c5c6): locates blob regions of value 3; within each blob, cells of value 2 expand outward to fill the blob; non-2 non-3 cells remain unchanged.

connect_markers_to_blob (task d43fd935): single-cell markers outside a blob are connected to the blob boundary by drawing a line segment (horizontal or vertical) from the marker to the nearest blob edge cell.

extend_period_pattern_shifted (task caa06a1f): a periodic row or column pattern (period P) detected in part of the grid is extended with a phase shift to fill the remaining zero rows or columns.

frame_via_markers (task 928ad970): four single-cell corner markers define the corners of a rectangular frame; the frame perimeter is drawn using those corner positions and the non-zero marker color.

grid_cell_hflip (task 9f236235): each individual cell of the grid is horizontally flipped in place; cells are replaced by their left-right mirror value from the same row.

l_shapes_to_quads (task a61ba2ce): L-shaped three-cell connected components of non-zero color are extended to fill a 2x2 quadrant; the missing fourth cell of each L is added using the same color.

WAVE 43 RULE ADDITIONS (2026-06-19)

Four new arc_transform rules added to arc_benchmark.pl in Mentova repo, feature/arc-wave42 branch (combined with wave 42). Three of four fired in benchmark Run 52.

Rules added:

colored_lines_sort (task 8e1813be): non-background colors each appear as a full horizontal or vertical line; lines are sorted by their position (row index or column index); output is an N x N grid of N solid-color rows or columns in sorted order; background value 5 distinguishes the separator pattern.

stamp_frame_colorize (task 9aec4887): a hollow rectangular frame with four distinct edge colors plus an interior 8-pattern; for each interior 8-cell the distance to each of four frame edges (top, bottom, left, right) is computed; the cell is assigned the color of the nearest edge; ties keep the pattern color. Rule added but did not fire in Run 52.

merge_sym_patterns (task c8cbb738): background is the most common color; each non-background color has exactly four cells forming a rectangle (corners only) or diamond (cardinal points) centered at the grid center; the output is a square of side 2*max_half+1 with all patterns superimposed.

stamp_into_5blocks (task e76a88a6): one non-zero non-5 source region plus N solid rectangular blocks of 5s all with the same dimensions; each 5-block is replaced by the corresponding source region cells using coordinate offset matching; BFS helpers sib_find_comps/sib_bfs identify connected components of 5-cells.

Helpers added for wave 43:
msp_hit/5 - checks whether a cell (Or, Oc) hits a rect or diamond shape at center Ctr with half-extents DR, DC.

sib_find_comps/5 - recursively finds all connected components of 5-valued cells via BFS seeds.
sib_bfs/6 - BFS expansion over 4-connected 5-valued cells given a queue and visited set.
sib_src_val/7 - maps a grid cell in a 5-block component to its corresponding source region value.

Part REF-W44: ARC-AGI-1 Wave 44 Named Rules

Wave 44 adds four arc_transform rules targeting failing ARC-AGI-1 tasks.

Three of four rules fired; score improves from 322/400 to 325/400 = 81.25%.

Rules added:

enclosed_1s_to_8 (task b2862040): background is 9; a BFS from all boundary 9-cells expands through 4-connected 9-neighbors to find the exterior 9-cells; 9-cells not reached are enclosed; 1-valued connected components that adjoin at least one enclosed 9-cell are recolored to 8 in the output.

snap_5s_to_block (task a48eeaf7): a solid 2x2 block of 2-cells is located; the adjacency ring (one step outside the 2x2) is computed; each 5-singleton maps to the nearest ring cell by Manhattan distance (lex tie-break on row, col); in the output moved 5s land at their ring target and original 5 positions become 0.

l_shape_compact (task 98cf29f8): exactly two non-zero colors are present; one forms a solid rectangle (anchor) and the other forms an L-shape; the L-shape is decomposed into a single-cell-wide arm and a wider rectangular block; the wide block is shifted along the arm direction by the arm length so it sits adjacent to the anchor; arm cells are cleared.

five_2x2_to_8_else_2 (task 150deff5): placeholder rule; did not fire because the actual task pattern (maximal independent set of non-overlapping 2x2 all-5 blocks) is more complex than the rule implements.

Helpers added for wave 44:
e1t8_bfs/6 - BFS expansion over 4-connected 9-valued cells starting from boundary seeds to find exterior 9-cells.
e1t8_comps/5 - finds all 4-connected components of 1-valued cells via BFS.
e1t8_comp_bfs/6 - BFS expansion over 1-valued cells for component finding.
e1t8_encloses_check/2 - checks whether a 1-component is adjacent to any enclosed 9-cell.
s5b_nearest/4 - selects the nearest ring cell to a given 5-cell by Manhattan distance.
lsc_is_solid_rect/1 - verifies that a set of cells exactly fills its bounding box.
lsc_separate/4 - decomposes an L-shape into arm and wide block with arm direction (vertical/horizontal).
lsc_move_block/5 - shifts the wide block by arm length in the arm direction.

Part REF-W45: Wave 45 ARC-AGI-1 Named Rules

Wave 45 adds four new named rules to arc_benchmark.pl. All four fired in the benchmark run, raising the score from 325/400 = 81.25% to 329/400 = 82.25%.

Rule cross_tile (task e21d9049):
The input grid is mostly zero with a + cross pattern of non-zero cells. The center cell is at the intersection of the horizontal and vertical arms. The rule tiles the center row with the horizontal arm sequence repeated cyclically, and the center column with the vertical arm sequence repeated cyclically. The tiling offset is determined by the position of the arm relative to the grid.
Helpers: ct_collect/3, ct_row_cells/4, ct_find_center/3, ct_count_row/3, ct_count_col/3, ct_arm_row/3, ct_arm_col/3, ct_make_row/10, ct_cell/10.

Rule frame_extract (task c909285e):
The input grid contains a repeating background pattern with a rectangular frame of a special color embedded in it. The frame forms a complete closed perimeter (cell count equals 2*(width-1) + 2*(height-1)). The rule detects the frame color and bounding box, then outputs a smaller grid containing the frame-colored border with the original interior pattern values.
Helpers: fe_collect/3, fe_row_cells/4, fe_find_frame/6, fe_build/7.

Rule sort_shapes_size (task f8ff0b80):
The input grid has a zero background with two or more distinctly colored shapes. Each color appears in exactly one connected region. The rule counts the number of cells per color, sorts colors by count descending, and outputs a single-column list with one color per row.
Helpers: sss_collect/3, sss_row_cells/4, sss_count_colors/2.

Rule mirror_fill_zero (task 9ecd008a):
The input grid is a symmetric patterned grid (fully non-zero) with a rectangular region replaced by zeros. The rule locates the zero-region bounding box, verifies it exactly fills the box, then fills each zero cell using the horizontally mirrored cell (column NC-1-C) from the same row.
Helpers: mfz_zeros/3, mfz_row_zeros/4.

All wave 45 arc_transform clauses end with ! and include NR =< 30, NC =< 30 size guards.

Acceptance criteria for wave 45:
AC-W45-001: arc_transform(cross_tile, ...) matches all training pairs of task e21d9049.

AC-W45-004: arc_transform(mirror_fill_zero, ...) matches all training pairs of task 9ecd008a.

Part REF-W46: Wave 46 Named Rules — zero_comp_size_to_color, denoise_stripes

Why these rules: Wave 46 targets two new ARC-AGI-1 task classes identified by analysis of
the remaining 71 failing tasks after wave 45. Both rules are deterministic, use only
standard arithmetic and list operations, and include size guards.

Rule zero_comp_size_to_color (task e8593010):
The input grid has a uniform non-zero background color (e.g. value 5) with scattered
zero-valued holes. The zero-cells form connected components under 4-connectivity. The
rule uses a BFS to find each connected component of zeros, assigns a color based on
component size: size 1 -> color 3, size 2 -> color 2, size 3 -> color 1. All
background cells retain their original value.
Helpers: zcs_collect_zeros/3, zcs_row_zeros/4, zcs_find_all_comps/5, zcs_bfs/6.

Rule denoise_stripes (task e26a3af2):
The input grid contains parallel color stripes (horizontal or vertical) contaminated
with randomly scattered noise pixels. The rule computes the mode (plurality color) of
each row and each column, then counts "violations" (cells differing from their stripe
mode) for both orientations. The orientation with fewer violations is used. Each row
(horizontal stripes) or each column (vertical stripes) is filled uniformly with its
mode color. A validity check requires at least 2 distinct stripe colors and the
violation count must not exceed 30% of total cells.
Helpers: ds_transpose/2, ds_mode/2, ds_row_violations/3, ds_col_violations/3.

All wave 46 arc_transform clauses end with ! and include NR =< 30, NC =< 30 size guards.

Acceptance criteria for wave 46:
AC-W46-001: arc_transform(zero_comp_size_to_color, ...) matches all training pairs of task e8593010.
AC-W46-002: arc_transform(denoise_stripes, ...) matches all training pairs of task e26a3af2.
AC-W46-003: All wave 46 arc_transform clauses end with ! and include NR =< 30, NC =< 30 size guards.

Wave 48 ARC-AGI-1 named-rule additions (2026-06-19):

Two new named induction rules were added to arc_benchmark.pl at line 23415.

Rule 1 - color_5comps_size6 (task d2abd087):
Finds all 4-connected components of value-5 cells in the input grid.
Components of size exactly 6 are recolored to 2 in the output.
Components of any other size are recolored to 1.
Guard: input must contain only 0-values and 5-values (no other colors).
Helpers: w48_five_cells/3, w48_five_row/4, w48_comps/5, w48_bfs/6.

Rule 2 - parity_5_to_3 (task d406998b):
Applies a column-parity test to every value-5 cell.
stay_parity = NC mod 2, where NC is the grid width.
A 5 at column c stays 5 if c mod 2 == stay_parity; otherwise it becomes 3.
All other cell values are left unchanged.
Guard: input must contain only 0-values and 5-values.

Wave 49 ARC-AGI-1 named-rule additions (2026-06-19):

Rule 1: classify_3shapes_by_turns (task e509e548).
Input has only 0s and 3s. Recolor each 4-connected component of value-3 cells by structural topology:
- A branch cell is any cell with 3 or more 4-connected neighbors within the same component.
- A corner cell is any cell that has both a horizontal neighbor and a vertical neighbor within the component.
- If any branch cell exists in the component: recolor all cells in that component to 2.
- If no branch cell and exactly 2 corner cells: recolor to 6.
- If no branch cell and exactly 1 corner cell: recolor to 1.
Helper predicates use w49_ prefix and are shared with Rule 2: w49_nz_cells, w49_nz_row, w49_comps, w49_bfs.

Rule 2: extend_staircase_bar (task 90f3ed37).
Input has only 0s and 8s. The key insight: the visual bar pattern consists of multiple 4-connected components
that are NOT individually connected but form a "row group" - maximal consecutive non-zero rows.
Algorithm:
1. Find all non-zero row indices and cluster into consecutive row groups (no all-zero row gap within a group).
2. The complete group is the unique group that has at least one row with an 8 at the rightmost column (NC-1).
3. Extract the template: for each row in the complete group, record (row_offset, col) for each 8-cell,
   where row_offset = abs_row - group_top_row.
4. For each incomplete group (no row reaches NC-1):
   - Compute global max_col = max over all column indices of all 8-cells in the entire group.
   - For each template cell (row_offset, col) where col > global_max_col:
     - Target row = incomplete_group_top + row_offset
     - If target cell is currently 0 in the grid, place value 1 there.
Helper predicates: w49_cluster_rows/2, w49_cluster_acc/4 (for row grouping).
The row-group approach was necessary because in the test input the complete "staircase" pattern
consists of three disconnected 4-components (rows 1 and 3 each reach NC-1 separately).

Acceptance criteria for wave 49:
AC-W49-001: arc_transform(classify_3shapes_by_turns, ...) matches all training pairs of task e509e548.
AC-W49-002: arc_transform(extend_staircase_bar, ...) matches all training pairs of task 90f3ed37.
AC-W49-003: All wave 49 arc_transform clauses end with ! and include NR =< 30, NC =< 30 size guards.
AC-W49-004: Full 400-task benchmark score 336/400 = 84.00% confirmed.

Score improvement: 334/400 = 83.50% to 336/400 = 84.00% (+2 tasks, Wave 49).

Status as of 2026-06-19: COMPLETE. Wave 49 on Mentova feature/arc-wave49 branch, merged via PR.


Wave 50 ARC-AGI-1 named-rule additions (2026-06-19):

Rule 1: border_9block_with_shadow (task db93a21d).
Input has only 0s and 9s. Each connected rectangular block of 9s is decorated with:
1. A 3-border (value 3) surrounding it with thickness T = max(block_height, block_width) // 2.
   The border ring is clamped to grid bounds on all sides.
2. A 1-shadow (value 1) extending downward from one row below the border bottom to the grid bottom,
   occupying the same column range as the 9-block itself.
When two changes overlap (a 3-border cell and a 1-shadow from different blocks), value 3 takes priority.
If the border bottom is at or beyond the last grid row, no shadow is emitted for that block.
Helper predicates: w50_block_groups/5, w50_bfs9/6 (shared 4-connected BFS for 9-cells).

Rule 2: stamp_cross_with_bridges (task f35d900a).
Input has exactly 4 non-zero cells with exactly 2 distinct values (call them A and B).
The 4 cells always form a rectangle with each opposite diagonal pair having the same value.
Algorithm:
1. For each non-zero cell with value V, stamp a 3x3 ring of the OPPOSITE value (A->B, B->A)
   around the cell; center cell retains its original value V.
2. For each pair of non-zero cells sharing the same row (same-row pair):
   - The gap between their stamp edges is from column C1+2 to column C2-2 (where C1 < C2).
   - 5-bridges are placed at alternating positions starting simultaneously from both ends
     (GS and GE) with step 2 inward until the two fronts cross.
3. For each pair of non-zero cells sharing the same column (same-col pair):
   - The gap is from row R1+2 to row R2-2 (where R1 < R2).
   - Same alternating-from-both-ends algorithm for 5-bridge placement.
Priority: original non-zero values > stamp ring > 5-bridges.
Helper predicates: w50_gap_cells/3, w50_gap_acc/3 (simultaneous-front alternating gap fill).

Acceptance criteria for wave 50:
AC-W50-001: arc_transform(border_9block_with_shadow, ...) matches all training pairs of task db93a21d.
AC-W50-002: arc_transform(stamp_cross_with_bridges, ...) matches all training pairs of task f35d900a.
AC-W50-003: All wave 50 arc_transform clauses end with ! and include NR =< 30, NC =< 30 size guards.
AC-W50-004: Full 400-task benchmark score 338/400 = 84.50% confirmed.

Score improvement: 336/400 = 84.00% to 338/400 = 84.50% (+2 tasks, Wave 50).

Status as of 2026-06-19: COMPLETE. Wave 50 on Mentova feature/arc-wave50 branch, merged via PR.

WAVE 51 - ARC-AGI-1 benchmark advancement

Rule 1: staircase_from_8.
Solves task d06dbe63. Identifies the seed value 8 in the input and grows a staircase pattern:
each row i (0-indexed) from the seed row gets all cells from column 0 to column i set to 8.
Passes all training pairs and test case.

Rule 2: mark_2x2_zero_blocks.
Solves task a8d7556c. Grid has only 0s and 5s; 5-cells are fixed. For each 4-connected zero
component, find the maximum area of any all-zero rectangle (height >= 2, width >= 2) within
the component using row-pair enumeration and run-finding. Mark all cells that belong to any
rectangle achieving the maximum area with value 2. Uses connected-component BFS (w51b_bfs)
and maximal-rectangle search (w51b_max_rect, w51b_runs).
Passes all training pairs and test case.

Rule 3: fill_rect_frame_interior (task e73095fd).
Grid has only 0s and 5s. Fills 0-cells enclosed by a rectangular frame of 5-cells with 4.
Grid boundary counts as a wall on the left or right side (not top or bottom). Passes all three
training pairs but fails the test case due to a spurious boundary-adjacent enclosure in the
test grid; does not contribute a point. Kept in code for future refinement.
New helpers: w51c_enclosed, w51c_row_all5, w51c_col_all5, w51c_interior_all0.

Acceptance criteria for wave 51:
AC-W51-001: arc_transform(staircase_from_8, ...) matches all training pairs of task d06dbe63.

WAVE 52 - ARC-AGI-1 benchmark advancement

Rule 1 (dead code): split_5s_by_2x2 (task 150deff5).
Attempted to distinguish 5-cells in any 2x2 all-5 block (mark 8) from isolated 5-cells (mark 2).
The algorithm finds cells belonging to ANY 2x2 all-5 block, but the real rule requires the
MAXIMUM INDEPENDENT SET of non-overlapping 2x2 blocks. Not yet solved. Dead code kept in
arc_benchmark.pl; fails all training pairs so arc_induce_rule_400 never applies it.

Rule 2: mark_zero_lines (task c1d99e64).
Grid contains non-zero values plus entire rows and/or columns that are all-0. The rule
identifies every all-zero row and every all-zero column, then replaces those cells with 2;
all other cells are unchanged. At least one zero-row or zero-col must exist; a fully-zero
grid is excluded. Bug fix during development: findall must use once/1 to emit each row index
exactly once when testing the non-zero membership condition.

Rule 3: tile_3row_pattern (task 8eb1be9a).
Exactly 3 consecutive non-zero rows form a tile; all other rows are entirely zero. The tile
is repeated (modulo-3 offset from the first tile row) to fill every row in the grid.
Guards: grid must have NR =< 30, exactly 3 consecutive non-zero rows, no other non-zero rows.
Bug fix during development: findall must use once/1 inside the generator to collect each row
index exactly once.

Acceptance criteria for wave 52:

WAVE 53 - ARC-AGI-1 benchmark advancement

Rule 1: rail_staircase_8s (task f15e1fac).
Input contains a single non-zero value (8) in an anchor pattern. The rule grows a filled
staircase: row at offset i from the topmost anchor row is filled from column 0 through
column i with value 8. The staircase fans downward and to the right.

Rule 2: shift_parallelogram_top (task 025d127b).
One or more parallelogram shapes of non-zero colors. For each color, the bottommost row
and the rightmost cell of that bottom row (the anchor) are fixed; all other cells shift
one column to the right. Converts a slanted parallelogram toward a more vertical shape.

Rule 3: reflect_5s_through_frame (task f8a8fe49).
A rectangular frame of 2-cells encloses 5-cells. If the top edge is completely filled
with 2s, reflection is vertical (each 5-cell maps across the nearer frame boundary
top/bottom); otherwise horizontal (maps across left/right frame boundary). Original
5-cells removed; reflected positions filled. Key check: forall over column range for
top-edge completeness.

Rule 4: diagonal_staircase_bounce (task a78176bb).
A diagonal of V-cells (constant col-minus-row = D) with 5-staircase markers on each
side. Right staircase (5s with col-row > D): new diagonal placed at D + max_right + 2.
Left staircase (5s with col-row < D): new diagonal at D - max_left - 2. All 5-cells
removed; original V-diagonal retained. Helper prefix w53d_.

Acceptance criteria for wave 53:
AC-W53-001: arc_transform(rail_staircase_8s, ...) matches all training pairs of f15e1fac.

WAVE 54 - ARC-AGI-1 benchmark advancement

Rule 1: overlay_halves_at_5sep (task e98196ab).
Input has an all-5 separator row exactly in the middle. Top half (above separator) and bottom
half (below separator) are overlaid cell-wise: if the top cell is nonzero, use it; otherwise
use the bottom cell. No position may have both halves nonzero (conflict guard). Output is the
half-sized grid.

Rule 2: repair_occluded_5x5_block (tasks dc0a314f and ff805c23).
A non-zero color forms a 5x5 solid rectangular block masking part of a globally symmetric
grid. Either the horizontal flip (h-flip: new_col = NC-1-(c0+dc)) or the vertical flip
(v-flip: new_row = NR-1-(r0+dr)) of the 5x5 block position gives an unoccluded mirror
patch. Output is the 5x5 reconstruction read from that unoccluded mirror patch.
dc0a314f uses occluder color 3; ff805c23 uses occluder color 1. One rule handles both.

WAVE 55 - ARC-AGI-1 benchmark advancement

Rule 1: repair_4fold_noise (task b8825c91).
Input has exactly two non-zero values: a noise value N (sparse, scattered) and a signal
value S (organized with 4-fold symmetry). Identification: pick N such that removing
all N-cells leaves a grid with 180-degree and horizontal-flip symmetry at every non-N cell.
For each N-cell, replace it with the first available non-N value from its three mirrors
(horizontal flip, vertical flip, full rotation). Original N-cells replaced; S-cells kept.

Rule 2: downscale_3x3_block_grid (task 5ad4f10b).
Input has exactly two non-zero colors: a shape color (organized into 3x3 rectangular
blocks) and a noise color (scattered). Shape is identified by higher cell density
(cells / bbox area) using cross-multiplication to avoid floating point. Bbox of shape
cells is divided into 3x3 equal blocks; each block outputs the noise color if a majority
of its cells are shape color, else 0. Output is always 3x3.
Key fix from initial implementation: density-based detection (N1 * Area2 >= N2 * Area1)
replaces count-based detection, which failed when noise outnumbers shape cells.

Acceptance criteria for wave 55:
AC-W55-001: arc_transform(repair_4fold_noise, ...) matches all training pairs of b8825c91.
AC-W55-002: arc_transform(downscale_3x3_block_grid, ...) matches all training pairs of 5ad4f10b.

WAVE 56 - ARC-AGI-1 benchmark advancement

Rule 1: fill_rect_frame_interiors (task e73095fd).
Input grids have 0s and 5s. The 5-cells form rectangular frames (all four sides fully
filled with 5s) or boundary-hugging frames (one open side reaches the grid edge).
Interior 0-cells of each frame are replaced with 4 in the output. Three frame cases
are handled:
  Case 1 - full rectangular frame: all four sides fully 5-filled. Fill interior with 4.
  Case 2 - right-boundary frame: left vertical wall + top and bottom rows extending to
    the last column; exact-width guard: grid[r1][c1-1] and grid[r2][c1-1] must not be 5.
    Fill interior (rows r1+1..r2-1, cols c1+1..NC-1) with 4.
  Case 3 - left-boundary frame: right vertical wall + top and bottom rows extending from
    col 0; exact-width guard: grid[r1][c2+1] and grid[r2][c2+1] must not be 5.
    Fill interior (rows r1+1..r2-1, cols 0..c2-1) with 4.
Note: the old wave 51 rule fill_rect_frame_interior (without the plural 's') had the same
task but a false-positive boundary-frame bug. It was removed and replaced by this rule.

Acceptance criteria for wave 56:
AC-W56-001: arc_transform(fill_rect_frame_interiors, ...) matches all training pairs of e73095fd.
AC-W56-002: The test case for e73095fd produces the correct output with no false positives.

WAVE 57 RULES

Wave 57 adds three new named transformation rules to arc_benchmark.pl.

Rule A: fill_zero_near_one (task 9edfc990).

Input: a noisy grid with non-zero values scattered throughout and some zero cells mixed in.

The grid also contains value-1 cells scattered at various positions.

The zero cells are 4-connected into multiple disconnected components.

Each zero component is classified by whether any cell in that component has a 4-adjacent neighbor whose value is 1.

If a zero component has at least one value-1 neighbor it is filled with 1 in the output.

If a zero component has no value-1 neighbor it stays 0 in the output.

Non-zero cells are unchanged.

Rule B: gravity_to_matching_wall (task d687bc17).

Input: a rectangular room with four distinct wall colors: top row (one color), bottom row (another color), left column (third color), right column (fourth color).

Corner cells are 0.

Interior cells (rows 2 to NR-1, cols 2 to NC-1) may contain scattered non-zero values.

Each interior non-zero value is compared to the four wall colors.

If the value matches the left wall color it moves to col 2 of the same row (adjacent to left wall).

If it matches the right wall color it moves to col NC-1 of the same row.

If it matches the top wall color it moves to row 2 of the same column.

If it matches the bottom wall color it moves to row NR-1 of the same column.

If it does not match any wall color it is erased (becomes 0).

The wall cells themselves are unchanged.

Rule C: key_masked_by_block_pattern (task 6ecd11f4).

Input: a large grid with two sub-regions.

The first sub-region is a regular NxM meta-grid of uniform blocks: each block is either filled entirely with a single repeated color (the block color) or is entirely 0.

The block color is the most frequent non-zero value in the grid.

The second sub-region is a small NxM grid of varied colored values (the key).

The key and block regions are in separate areas of the grid, separated by zeros.

The output is an NxM grid: for each meta-position (i,j), the output cell is key(i,j) if block(i,j) is filled, else 0.

Acceptance criteria for wave 57:
AC-W57-001: arc_transform(fill_zero_near_one, ...) matches all three training pairs of 9edfc990.
AC-W57-002: The test case for 9edfc990 produces the correct output.
AC-W57-003: arc_transform(gravity_to_matching_wall, ...) matches all three training pairs of d687bc17.
AC-W57-004: The test case for d687bc17 produces the correct output.
AC-W57-005: arc_transform(key_masked_by_block_pattern, ...) matches all three training pairs of 6ecd11f4.
AC-W57-006: The test case for 6ecd11f4 produces the correct output.
AC-W57-007: Full 400-task benchmark score 355/400 = 88.75% confirmed (3 new tasks, Wave 57).

Score improvement: 352/400 = 88.00% to 355/400 = 88.75% (+3 tasks, Wave 57).

Status as of 2026-06-20: COMPLETE. Wave 57 on Mentova feature/wave-57 branch, merged via PR.


Part 36 Section 36.8: Wave 58 ARC-AGI-1 Rules

Wave 58 added two new named rules to arc_benchmark.pl:

Rule A: box_extract_recolor_by_dots (task fcb5c309).

Input: a grid with exactly two non-zero colors. The more-frequent color forms rectangular outlines or closed shapes (the frame color). The less-frequent color is sparse dots scattered around the grid.

The output is the bounding box of the frame-color connected component that encloses the most dot-color cells. Every non-zero cell in that bounding box is recolored to the dot color. Zero cells stay zero.

Rule C: fill_grid_regions_by_line_holes (task 83302e8f).

Input: a grid where a single background value B (the most frequent non-zero value) forms a regular lattice of horizontal and vertical lines. All other cells are 0. Some line cells are holes (0 instead of B).

Output rules: B cells stay B. Zero cells on any line row or line col become 4 (marking the hole). Zero cells in content regions (off every line) become 4 if any of the four enclosing boundary line segments contains a hole, or 3 if all four boundary segments are intact.

Part 36 Section 36.9: Wave 59 ARC-AGI-1 Rules

Wave 59 added two new named rules to arc_benchmark.pl:

Rule A: fill_frame_interior_radiate (task aba27056).

Input: a grid with exactly one non-zero color forming a rectangular frame shape that has one open side (a contiguous run of 0-cells on one border wall of the bounding box).

Output: the frame color is preserved. All 0-cells strictly inside the bounding box are filled with 4. The open-side cells (the gap in the border wall) are also filled with 4. Then 4s radiate outward from the opening in a starburst pattern: at each step D away from the opening wall, the full opening-column (or opening-row) projection is repeated, and two expanding boundary tracks add one cell per step to each perpendicular side.

Rule B: complete_rotational_symmetry (task e40b9e2f).

Input: a grid with exactly two non-zero colors whose shape is incomplete under 4-fold (90-degree) rotational symmetry. The rotational centre is found by locating the pair of rows with identical non-zero patterns that are farthest apart; those rows give the centre row, and the pivot row between them (or the symmetric rows themselves for half-integer centres) gives the centre column via min/max non-zero column midpoint.

Output: the input is preserved. Each non-zero cell's three 90-degree CW rotational images around the computed centre are added with the same color value, filling any 0-cells at those positions.

Acceptance criteria for wave 59:
AC-W59-001: arc_transform(fill_frame_interior_radiate, ...) matches all training pairs of aba27056.
AC-W59-002: The test case for aba27056 produces the correct output.
AC-W59-003: arc_transform(complete_rotational_symmetry, ...) matches all training pairs of e40b9e2f.
AC-W59-004: The test case for e40b9e2f produces the correct output.
AC-W59-005: Full 400-task benchmark score 359/400 = 89.75% confirmed (2 new tasks, Wave 59).

Score improvement: 357/400 = 89.25% to 359/400 = 89.75% (+2 tasks, Wave 59).

Part 36 Section 36.10: Wave 60 ARC-AGI-1 Rules

Wave 60 added two new named rules to arc_benchmark.pl:

Rule A: extreme_region_fill (task 6455b5f5).

Input: a grid whose non-zero cells are all value 2, forming walls that enclose rectangular interior rooms filled with value 0. The rule uses flood-fill connected-component analysis to find all 4-connected components of 0-cells. It computes the cell count of each component, identifies the largest and smallest by count, fills the largest component with value 1, and fills the smallest component with value 8. Middle-sized components remain 0. All non-zero wall cells are unchanged. The rule requires at least two distinct 0-components with unequal sizes.

Rule B: diagonal_cavity_stamp (task e8dc4411).

Input: a grid with a background color B (the most frequent cell value), a cavity of 0-cells, and exactly one marker cell whose value M differs from B and from 0. The rule computes the centroid of the cavity cells, determines the diagonal direction D from centroid to marker using integer arithmetic to avoid floating-point, and finds the smallest step S such that the cavity shifted by S in direction D shares no cell with the original cavity. It then stamps copies of the cavity (painted with color M) at offsets 1*S*D, 2*S*D, and so on, adding only in-bounds cells, stopping when a full shift lands off-grid. The original cavity 0-cells and marker are preserved.

Acceptance criteria for wave 60:
AC-W60-001: arc_transform(extreme_region_fill, ...) matches all training pairs of 6455b5f5.
AC-W60-002: The test case for 6455b5f5 produces the correct output.
AC-W60-003: arc_transform(diagonal_cavity_stamp, ...) matches all training pairs of e8dc4411.
AC-W60-004: The test case for e8dc4411 produces the correct output.
AC-W60-005: Full 400-task benchmark score 361/400 = 90.25% confirmed (2 new tasks, Wave 60).

Score improvement: 359/400 = 89.75% to 361/400 = 90.25% (+2 tasks, Wave 60).

Status as of 2026-06-20: COMPLETE. Wave 60 on Mentova feature/arc-wave-60-rules branch, merged via PR.


Part 36 Section 36.11: Wave 61 ARC-AGI-1 Rules

Wave 61 added two new named rules to arc_benchmark.pl:

Rule A: concentric_square_rings (task 5c2c9af4).

Input: a grid with exactly N non-zero dots (N >= 2) all sharing one color C. The dots lie on a diagonal line with equal absolute row and column spacing s > 0. The rule identifies the middle dot as the center, then colors every output cell whose Chebyshev distance (max of absolute row and column offsets) from the center is exactly divisible by s; all other cells become 0. This produces concentric square rings of color C spaced s apart, centered on the middle dot.

Rule B: corner_ripple_even_chebyshev (task d22278a0).

Input: a grid where every non-zero cell sits at a corner of the grid (positions (1,1), (1,NC), (NR,1), or (NR,NC)). Each corner seed has a color value. For each output cell, the rule finds the nearest seed by Chebyshev distance; when multiple seeds are equidistant in Chebyshev, it breaks the tie using Manhattan distance; a tie unresolvable by Manhattan becomes 0. The cell takes the winning seed's color if the Chebyshev distance is even, and 0 if the distance is odd.

Acceptance criteria for wave 61:
AC-W61-001: arc_transform(concentric_square_rings, ...) matches all training pairs of 5c2c9af4.
AC-W61-002: The test case for 5c2c9af4 produces the correct output.
AC-W61-003: arc_transform(corner_ripple_even_chebyshev, ...) matches all training pairs of d22278a0.
AC-W61-004: The test case for d22278a0 produces the correct output.
AC-W61-005: Full 400-task benchmark score 363/400 = 90.75% confirmed (2 new tasks, Wave 61).

Score improvement: 361/400 = 90.25% to 363/400 = 90.75% (+2 tasks, Wave 61).

Part 36 Section 36.12: Wave 62 ARC-AGI-1 Rules

Wave 62 added two new named rules to arc_benchmark.pl:

Rule A: graybox_hole_fill_by_unique_shape (task 228f6490).

Input: a grid containing gray (value 5) rectangular regions with interior zero-cell holes, plus loose colored blobs scattered in the background. Each hole has a specific shape (normalized 2D cell pattern). Each blob has a color. For each color that appears as exactly one blob (a unique-color mover), the rule finds the interior hole whose shape matches the blob's normalized shape and fills the hole with the blob's color, then erases the blob. Distractor colors appearing as multiple blobs are left untouched. Holes with no matching unique-color blob are also unchanged.

Rule B: corner_nested_frame (task 9d9215db).

Input: a sparse 19x19 grid with a small cluster of non-zero cells concentrated in one corner quadrant. The cells form a nested frame seed: corner cells (where row-distance and column-distance from the nearest grid corner are equal) define the frame's corner values; arm cells (where those two distances differ by exactly 2) define the arm values. The rule reflects all cells to their four symmetric positions (horizontal, vertical, and diagonal), and fills each arm cell's row (and its mirror row) or column (and its mirror column) between the seed and its reflection using the arm's value at step 2. The result is a 4-fold symmetric nested rectangular frame drawn in the sparse grid.

Acceptance criteria for wave 62:
AC-W62-001: arc_transform(graybox_hole_fill_by_unique_shape, ...) matches all training pairs of 228f6490.
AC-W62-002: The test case for 228f6490 produces the correct output.
AC-W62-003: arc_transform(corner_nested_frame, ...) matches all training pairs of 9d9215db.
AC-W62-004: The test case for 9d9215db produces the correct output.
AC-W62-005: Full 400-task benchmark score 365/400 = 91.25% confirmed (2 new tasks, Wave 62).

Part 36 Section 36.13: Wave 63 ARC-AGI-1 Rules

Wave 63 added four new named rules to arc_benchmark.pl. Three of the four target tasks were already
solved by earlier rules; only task 150deff5 is a net new solve, raising the score to 366/400.

Rule A: concat_vflip (task 8be77c9e).

Input: any non-empty grid. The output is the original rows followed by the rows in reverse order
(vertical mirror appended below). The resulting output has twice as many rows as the input.
Note: this task was already solved by the earlier tile_reflect_v rule; concat_vflip is a valid
alternative rule retained for completeness.

Rule B: color_6_to_2 (task b1948b0a).

Input: a grid containing only cells with values 6 or 7 (no other non-zero values). Every cell
with value 6 is replaced by value 2; cells with value 7 are unchanged.
Note: this task was already solved by the swap recolor rule; color_6_to_2 is retained.

Rule C: extract_non1_bbox (task a740d043).

Input: a grid whose background is value 1 (no zero background). Find the tight bounding box of
all cells that are not 1. Extract that sub-grid, replacing any remaining 1-cells inside it with 0.
Note: this task was already solved by the crop_nonbg_bbox rule; extract_non1_bbox is retained.

Rule D: five_shape_fat_thin (task 150deff5).

Input: a grid with a connected shape made entirely of cells with value 5. Find the
maximum-size set of non-overlapping 2x2 all-5 blocks such that every remaining 5-cell
(one not covered by any selected block) has at least one 4-adjacent neighbor that is
also a remaining 5-cell (no isolated thin cells). Cells in selected blocks become 8;
remaining 5-cells become 2; all other cells stay 0. The search uses a greedy cut: the
first valid selection found (tried from largest to smallest, in row-major order) is used.

Acceptance criteria for wave 63:
AC-W63-001: arc_transform(concat_vflip, ...) matches all training pairs of 8be77c9e.
AC-W63-002: arc_transform(color_6_to_2, ...) matches all training pairs of b1948b0a.
